// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// NORMALIZATION MAPPINGS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const BRAND_MAP = {
  // Normalize brand strings to ALM uppercase names
  'gm': 'CHEVROLET', 'chevrolet': 'CHEVROLET',
  'volkswagen': 'VOLKSWAGEN', 'vw': 'VOLKSWAGEN',
  'fiat': 'FIAT', 'ford': 'FORD',
  'honda': 'HONDA', 'toyota': 'TOYOTA',
  'hyundai': 'HYUNDAI', 'renault': 'RENAULT',
  'peugeot': 'PEUGEOT', 'citroen': 'CITROËN', 'citroën': 'CITROËN',
  'nissan': 'NISSAN', 'mitsubishi': 'MITSUBISHI',
  'bmw': 'BMW', 'audi': 'AUDI',
  'jeep': 'JEEP', 'kia': 'KIA',
  'land rover': 'LAND ROVER', 'volvo': 'VOLVO',
  'chery': 'CHERY', 'cherry': 'CHERY',
  'dafra': 'DAFRA',
};


const COLOR_MAP = {
  'branca': 5, 'branco': 5,
  'preta': 18, 'preto': 18, 'preto onix': 19,
  'cinza': 11, 'cinza-escuro': 13, 'grafite': 13,
  'prata': 17,
  'azul': 2,
  'vermelho': 24, 'vermelha': 24,
  'verde': 23,
  'amarelo': 1, 'amarela': 1,
  'marrom': 16,
  'bege': 3,
  'laranja': 15,
  'bordo': 4,
  'roxo': 21,
  'rosa': 20,
  'vinho': 25,
  'dourado': 12, 'dourada': 12,
  'bronze': 7,
  'champagne': 9,
  'chumbo': 10,
  'grena': 14,
  'uva': 22,
};


const FUEL_MAP = {
  'gasolina': 1,
  'flex': 2,
  'álcool': 3, 'alcool': 3, 'gasolina e álcool': 3,
  'gnv': 4,
  'diesel': 5,
  'elétrico': 6, 'eletrico': 6,
};


const CAMBIO_MAP = {
  'manual': 1,
  'automático': 2, 'automatico': 2,
  'semi-automático': 3, 'semi-automatico': 3, 'automatizado': 3,
  'cvt': 3,
};


const TYPE_MAP = {
  'carro': 'Carro',
  'moto': 'Moto',
  'caminhonete': 'Carro',
  'van': 'Carro',
};


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// OVERRIDE STORE — user corrections persisted in memory
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
const overrides = {};


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MATCHING FUNCTIONS
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function normStr(s) {
  return (s||'').toLowerCase().trim().normalize('NFD').replace(/[\u0300-\u036f]/g,'').replace(/[-_]/g,' ').replace(/\s+/g,' ').trim();
}


function matchBrand(brandStr, vehicleType) {
  const norm = normStr(brandStr);
  const mapped = BRAND_MAP[norm];
  if (!mapped) return null;
  const isMoto = (vehicleType || '').toLowerCase() === 'moto';
  if (isMoto) {
    const motoBrand = ALM_MARCAS.find(m => m.nome === mapped && m.tipo === 'Moto');
    if (motoBrand) return motoBrand;
  }
  return ALM_MARCAS.find(m => m.nome === mapped && m.tipo !== 'Moto') || ALM_MARCAS.find(m => m.nome === mapped) || null;
}


function matchModel(brandId, modelStr) {
  const norm = normStr(modelStr);
  const models = ALM_MODELOS.filter(m => m.marcaId === brandId);
  if (!models.length) return null;
  // exact match
  let match = models.find(m => normStr(m.nome) === norm);
  if (match) return match;
  // partial match
  match = models.find(m => normStr(m.nome).includes(norm) || norm.includes(normStr(m.nome)));
  return match || null;
}


function matchColor(colorStr) {
  const norm = normStr(colorStr);
  const id = COLOR_MAP[norm];
  if (id) return ALM_CORES.find(c => c.id === id);
  // try partial
  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(COLOR_MAP)) {
    if (norm.includes(k) || k.includes(norm)) return ALM_CORES.find(c => c.id === v);
  }
  return null;
}


function matchFuel(fuelStr) {
  const norm = normStr(fuelStr);
  const id = FUEL_MAP[norm];
  if (id) return ALM_COMBUSTIVEIS.find(c => c.id === id);
  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(FUEL_MAP)) {
    if (norm.includes(k)) return ALM_COMBUSTIVEIS.find(c => c.id === v);
  }
  return null;
}


function matchCambio(trans) {
  const norm = normStr(trans);
  const id = CAMBIO_MAP[norm];
  if (id) return ALM_CAMBIOS.find(c => c.id === id);
  return null;
}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MAP VEHICLE → ALM
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function mapVehicle(v) {
  const id = v.id;
  const ov = overrides[id] || {};
  
  let brandMatch  = matchBrand(ov.brand || v.brand, ov.vehicle_type || v.vehicle_type);
  let modelMatch  = brandMatch ? matchModel(brandMatch.id, ov.model || v.model) : null;
  // Fallback: if model not found under carro brand, try moto brand (e.g. PCX registered as carro)
  if (brandMatch && !modelMatch) {
    const altBrand = ALM_MARCAS.find(m => m.nome === brandMatch.nome && m.tipo !== brandMatch.tipo);
    if (altBrand) {
      const altModel = matchModel(altBrand.id, ov.model || v.model);
      if (altModel) { brandMatch = altBrand; modelMatch = altModel; }
    }
  }
  const colorMatch  = matchColor(ov.color || v.color || '');
  const fuelMatch   = matchFuel(ov.fuel || v.fuel_type || '');
  const cambioMatch = matchCambio(ov.transmission || v.transmission || '');
  const tipoVeiculo = TYPE_MAP[normStr(v.vehicle_type||'carro')] || 'Carro';
  
  const issues = [];
  if (!brandMatch) issues.push('Marca não encontrada no ALM');
  if (brandMatch && !modelMatch) {
    const brandHasModels = ALM_MODELOS.some(m => m.marcaId === brandMatch.id);
    if (brandHasModels) {
      issues.push('Modelo não cadastrado no ALM — selecione manualmente ou cadastre no ALM');
    } else {
      issues.push('Marca sem modelos no ALM — adicione modelos no sistema ALM primeiro');
    }
  }
  if (!fuelMatch) issues.push('Combustível não mapeado');
  if (!cambioMatch) issues.push('Câmbio não mapeado');
  if (!v.sale_price) issues.push('Preço de venda em branco');
  
  let matchLevel = 'ok';
  if (issues.some(i => i.includes('Marca') || i.includes('Preço'))) matchLevel = 'err';
  else if (issues.length > 0) matchLevel = 'warn';
  
  return {
    raw: v,
    brandMatch, modelMatch, colorMatch, fuelMatch, cambioMatch,
    tipoVeiculo, issues, matchLevel,
    almPayload: buildPayload(v, brandMatch, modelMatch, colorMatch, fuelMatch, cambioMatch, tipoVeiculo)
  };
}


function buildPayload(v, brandMatch, modelMatch, colorMatch, fuelMatch, cambioMatch, tipoVeiculo) {
  return {
    TipoVeiculo: tipoVeiculo,
    StatusVeiculo: "Cadastrado",
    MarcaId: brandMatch ? brandMatch.id : null,
    ModeloId: modelMatch ? modelMatch.id : null,
    VersaoId: null,
    Placa: v.plate || '',
    Chassi: v.chassis || '',
    ZeroKm: false,
    Ano: parseInt(v.year_fabrication) || null,
    AnoModelo: parseInt(v.year_model) || null,
    Km: parseInt((v.km||'0').toString().replace(/\D/g,'')) || 0,
    NumeroDonos: null,
    QtdPortas: parseInt(v.doors) || null,
    Valor: parseFloat(v.sale_price) || 0,
    Descricao: v.notes || `${v.brand} ${v.model} ${v.version||''} - ${v.year_fabrication}/${v.year_model}`,
    CombustivelId: fuelMatch ? fuelMatch.id : null,
    CambioId: cambioMatch ? cambioMatch.id : null,
    CategoriaId: null,
    DirecaoId: null,
    CorId: colorMatch ? colorMatch.id : null,
    MotorId: null,
    PartidaId: null,
    AlimentacaoId: null,
    RefrigeracaoId: null,
    FreioId: null,
    TipoMotor: v.version || '',
    Cilindrada: null,
    opcionaisId: [],
    fotosId: []
  };
}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// RENDER
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
let mappedVehicles = [];


function updateStats() { renderTable(); }


function init() {
  mappedVehicles = RAW_VEHICLES.map(mapVehicle);
  buildMappingPanel();
  renderTable();
}


function renderTable() {
  const filterStatus = document.getElementById('filter-status').value;
  const filterMatch  = document.getElementById('filter-match').value;
  const search       = normStr(document.getElementById('filter-search').value);
  
  let filtered = mappedVehicles.filter(mv => {
    if (filterStatus !== 'all' && mv.raw.status !== filterStatus) return false;
    if (filterMatch !== 'all' && mv.matchLevel !== filterMatch) return false;
    if (search) {
      const haystack = normStr(`${mv.raw.brand} ${mv.raw.model} ${mv.raw.plate} ${mv.raw.version}`);
      if (!haystack.includes(search)) return false;
    }
    return true;
  });
  
  const counts = {ok:0, warn:0, err:0};
  mappedVehicles.forEach(mv => counts[mv.matchLevel]++);
  document.getElementById('count-ok').textContent = counts.ok;
  document.getElementById('count-warn').textContent = counts.warn;
  document.getElementById('count-err').textContent = counts.err;
  
  const ready = mappedVehicles.filter(mv => mv.matchLevel === 'ok' && mv.raw.status === 'disponivel').length;
  const warnReady = mappedVehicles.filter(mv => mv.matchLevel === 'warn' && mv.raw.status === 'disponivel').length;
  document.getElementById('export-ready').textContent = ready;
  const warnEl = document.getElementById('export-warn-count');
  if (warnEl) warnEl.textContent = warnReady;
  
  const tbody = document.getElementById('table-body');
  tbody.innerHTML = filtered.map((mv, idx) => {
    const v = mv.raw;
    const thumb = (v.images && v.images.length) 
      ? `<img src="${v.images[0]}" class="img-thumb" onerror="this.style.display='none'">`
      : `<span style="color:#ccc;font-size:18px">📷</span>`;
    
    const brandStr = mv.brandMatch 
      ? `<span style="color:#222">${v.brand}</span> → <b style="color:var(--green)">${mv.brandMatch.nome} [ID ${mv.brandMatch.id}]</b>`
      : `<span style="color:var(--red)">${v.brand} ❌</span>`;
    
    const modelStr = mv.modelMatch
      ? `<span style="color:#222">${v.model}</span> → <b style="color:var(--green)">${mv.modelMatch.nome} [ID ${mv.modelMatch.id}]</b>`
      : mv.brandMatch
        ? `<span style="color:#cc7700">${v.model} ⚠️</span><br><select class="field-edit warn" onchange="setModelOverride('${v.id}', this.value, this)" style="width:160px">
             <option value="">-- selecione --</option>
             ${ALM_MODELOS.filter(m=>m.marcaId===mv.brandMatch.id).map(m=>`<option value="${m.id}">${m.nome}</option>`).join('')}
             <option value="custom">+ Não listado (ignorar)</option>
           </select>`
        : `<span style="color:#ccc">${v.model}</span>`;
    
    const colorStr = mv.colorMatch
      ? `<b style="color:var(--green)">${mv.colorMatch.nome} [${mv.colorMatch.id}]</b>`
      : `<span style="color:#cc7700">${v.color||'—'} ⚠️</span>`;
    
    const fuelStr = mv.fuelMatch
      ? `<b style="color:var(--green)">${mv.fuelMatch.nome} [${mv.fuelMatch.id}]</b>`
      : `<span style="color:#cc7700">${v.fuel_type||'—'} ⚠️</span>`;
    
    const cambioStr = mv.cambioMatch
      ? `<b style="color:var(--green)">${mv.cambioMatch.nome} [${mv.cambioMatch.id}]</b>`
      : `<span style="color:#cc7700">${v.transmission||'—'} ⚠️</span>`;
    
    const statusBadge = v.status === 'disponivel'
      ? '<span class="status-badge s-ok">disponível</span>'
      : '<span class="status-badge s-vendido">vendido</span>';
    
    const matchBadge = mv.matchLevel === 'ok'
      ? '<span class="status-badge s-ok">✅ pronto</span>'
      : mv.matchLevel === 'warn'
      ? `<span class="status-badge s-warn" title="${mv.issues.join('; ')}">⚠️ atenção</span>`
      : `<span class="status-badge s-err" title="${mv.issues.join('; ')}">❌ erro</span>`;


    const price = v.sale_price ? `R$ ${parseFloat(v.sale_price).toLocaleString('pt-BR', {minimumFractionDigits:2})}` : '<span style="color:#ccc">—</span>';
    const typeTag = mv.tipoVeiculo === 'Carro' ? 'tag-carro' : 'tag-moto';
    
    return `<tr>
      <td><b>${idx+1}</b></td>
      <td>${thumb}</td>
      <td><span class="tag ${typeTag}">${mv.tipoVeiculo}</span></td>
      <td>${brandStr}</td>
      <td>${modelStr}</td>
      <td style="max-width:120px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap" title="${v.version||''}"><small>${v.version||'—'}</small></td>
      <td><b>${v.plate||'—'}</b></td>
      <td>${v.year_fabrication}/${v.year_model}</td>
      <td>${parseInt((v.km||0).toString().replace(/\D/g,'')).toLocaleString('pt-BR')}</td>
      <td>${colorStr}</td>
      <td>${fuelStr}</td>
      <td>${cambioStr}</td>
      <td>${price}</td>
      <td>${statusBadge}</td>
      <td>${matchBadge}</td>
    </tr>`;
  }).join('');
}


function setModelOverride(vehicleId, modelId, selectEl) {
  if (!modelId || modelId === 'custom') return;
  overrides[vehicleId] = overrides[vehicleId] || {};
  overrides[vehicleId].modelId = parseInt(modelId);
  // Recompute
  const mv = mappedVehicles.find(m => m.raw.id === vehicleId);
  if (mv) {
    const model = ALM_MODELOS.find(m => m.id === parseInt(modelId));
    mv.modelMatch = model;
    mv.almPayload.ModeloId = parseInt(modelId);
    if (mv.issues.length && mv.brandMatch) mv.matchLevel = 'ok';
  }
  selectEl.closest('td').innerHTML = `<b style="color:var(--green)">${ALM_MODELOS.find(m=>m.id===parseInt(modelId))?.nome} [ID ${modelId}]</b>`;
  const counts = {ok:0, warn:0, err:0};
  mappedVehicles.forEach(m => counts[m.matchLevel]++);
  document.getElementById('count-ok').textContent = counts.ok;
  document.getElementById('count-warn').textContent = counts.warn;
  const ready = mappedVehicles.filter(m => m.matchLevel === 'ok' && m.raw.status === 'disponivel').length;
  document.getElementById('export-ready').textContent = ready;
}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// MAPPING PANEL
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function buildMappingPanel() {
  const unmappedBrands = [...new Set(RAW_VEHICLES.map(v => v.brand).filter(b => !matchBrand(b)))];
  const unmappedColors = [...new Set(RAW_VEHICLES.map(v => v.color).filter(c => c && !matchColor(c)))];
  const unmappedFuels  = [...new Set(RAW_VEHICLES.map(v => v.fuel_type).filter(f => f && !matchFuel(f)))];
  const unmappedTrans  = [...new Set(RAW_VEHICLES.map(v => v.transmission).filter(t => t && !matchCambio(t)))];
  
  let html = '';
  
  unmappedBrands.forEach(brand => {
    html += `<div class="mapping-item">
      <label>Marca</label>
      <b>${brand}</b>
      <span class="arrow">→</span>
      <select onchange="addBrandMap('${brand}', this.value)" style="flex:1">
        <option value="">-- selecionar ALM --</option>
        ${ALM_MARCAS.slice(0,50).map(m=>`<option value="${m.nome}">${m.nome}</option>`).join('')}
      </select>
    </div>`;
  });
  
  unmappedColors.forEach(color => {
    html += `<div class="mapping-item">
      <label>Cor</label>
      <b>${color}</b>
      <span class="arrow">→</span>
      <select onchange="addColorMap('${color}', this.value)" style="flex:1">
        <option value="">-- selecionar --</option>
        ${ALM_CORES.map(c=>`<option value="${c.id}">${c.nome}</option>`).join('')}
      </select>
    </div>`;
  });
  
  if (unmappedBrands.length === 0 && unmappedColors.length === 0 && unmappedFuels.length === 0 && unmappedTrans.length === 0) {
    html = '<p style="color:var(--green);font-weight:700">✅ Todos os campos principais foram mapeados automaticamente!</p>';
  }
  
  document.getElementById('mapping-grid').innerHTML = html;
}


function addBrandMap(raw, almName) {
  if (!almName) return;
  BRAND_MAP[normStr(raw)] = almName;
  mappedVehicles = RAW_VEHICLES.map(mapVehicle);
  buildMappingPanel();
  renderTable();
}


function addColorMap(raw, almId) {
  if (!almId) return;
  COLOR_MAP[normStr(raw)] = parseInt(almId);
  mappedVehicles = RAW_VEHICLES.map(mapVehicle);
  buildMappingPanel();
  renderTable();
}


// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
// EXPORT
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
function getExportVehicles(onlyReady = true, onlyDisponivel = true) {
  const includeWarnEl = document.getElementById('include-warn');
  const includeWarn = includeWarnEl ? includeWarnEl.checked : false;
  return mappedVehicles
    .filter(mv => !onlyDisponivel || mv.raw.status === 'disponivel')
    .filter(mv => !onlyReady || mv.matchLevel === 'ok' || (includeWarn && mv.matchLevel === 'warn'))
    .map(mv => mv.almPayload);
}


function generateJSON() {
  const data = getExportVehicles(true, true);
  const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(data, null, 2)], {type: 'application/json'});
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  a.download = 'estoque_alm_export.json';
  a.click();
}


function generateXML() {
  const data = getExportVehicles(true, true);
  const xmlLines = ['<?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8"?>', '<Veiculos>'];
  data.forEach(v => {
    xmlLines.push('  <Veiculo>');
    for (const [key, val] of Object.entries(v)) {
      if (Array.isArray(val)) {
        xmlLines.push(`    <${key}>${val.join(',')}</${key}>`);
      } else if (val !== null && val !== undefined) {
        xmlLines.push(`    <${key}>${String(val).replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;')}</${key}>`);
      } else {
        xmlLines.push(`    <${key}></${key}>`);
      }
    }
    xmlLines.push('  </Veiculo>');
  });
  xmlLines.push('</Veiculos>');
  const blob = new Blob([xmlLines.join('\n')], {type: 'application/xml'});
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  a.download = 'estoque_alm_export.xml';
  a.click();
}


function exportCSV() {
  const data = getExportVehicles(false, false);
  const headers = Object.keys(data[0] || {});
  const rows = [headers.join(';')];
  data.forEach(v => {
    rows.push(headers.map(h => {
      const val = v[h];
      if (Array.isArray(val)) return val.join(',');
      if (val === null || val === undefined) return '';
      return String(val).replace(/;/g, ',');
    }).join(';'));
  });
  const blob = new Blob([rows.join('\n')], {type: 'text/csv;charset=utf-8'});
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
  a.download = 'estoque_alm_export.csv';
  a.click();
}


function previewExport() {
  const data = getExportVehicles(true, true);
  document.getElementById('modal-title').textContent = `Preview JSON — ${data.length} veículos prontos para importação`;
  document.getElementById('modal-content').textContent = JSON.stringify(data.slice(0,3), null, 2) + (data.length > 3 ? `\n\n... e mais ${data.length - 3} veículos` : '');
  document.getElementById('modal-dl-btn').onclick = generateJSON;
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.add('open');
}


function closeModal() {
  document.getElementById('modal').classList.remove('open');
}


init();
</script>
</body>
</html>
